posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:After doing a lot of comparisons on a certain book and Ctrip, I chose this one. It usually takes about 20 minutes to get there by taxi from the airport (there was a bit of traffic when I went there, so I could get there in about 30 minutes). First of all, the location is very good, right next to the beach of Zengcuo'an. You can see the beach in 1 minute when you go out, but it is not directly facing the beach. It is hidden on the second side, which gives you a feeling of quietness in the hustle and bustle. The transportation is very convenient. There are two stations outside, which can go directly to Xiamen University and the cruise terminal. If the traffic on the road is congested during holidays, it is also a good choice to take a bus and slowly enjoy the scenery along the way. This time I stayed in a double room, without sea view. The room is quite large, and two people can walk around in it without affecting each other. The bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, with a shower and a bathtub, and the toilet is an automatic sensor toilet. The wash basin does have the problems mentioned in other reviews. The faucet is too short, and water will splash out when washing hands. The two sinks next to the basin are full of water and will flow to the ground. There is basically no problem if you put a floor towel on the two corners of the ground. The breakfast is also good. I recommend beef brisket noodles and shacha seafood noodles (noodles are better than noodles). The dishes are replenished quite promptly. I was worried that there would be too many guests staying in the hotel during the holidays and the service would not be able to keep up. It turned out that my worries were unnecessary. The overall experience was very good, and the local restaurants recommended by the hotel were also very delicious. The only shortcoming is that the sanitary dead corners need to be fixed, but everything else is good.

The hotel has not been open for a long time, and all the facilities are brand new. The lobby and rooms are designed in a simple and modern style, fully reflecting the characteristics of Hilton Curio, a resort brand. In particular, there is a Starbucks on the first floor of the hotel, which is definitely a blessing for coffee lovers. Although the infinity swimming pool on the third floor of the hotel is not large in size, it is also a good place to cool off from the summer heat by lying beside the pool and watching the night view.
The service of the staff also reflects the consistent standard of Hilton, which is civilized and polite without losing enthusiasm, and all guests are very satisfied.
I will definitely stay here next time I come to Xiamen!
